│   │   │       --- Start of about.js ---
│   │   │       document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
│   │   │           const aboutItems = document.querySelectorAll('.about-section');
│   │   │       
│   │   │           aboutItems.forEach(item => {
│   │   │               const question = item.querySelector('.about-question');
│   │   │       
│   │   │               question.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │   │                   // Toggle the active class
│   │   │                   item.classList.toggle('active');
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Close other open about items (optional)
│   │   │                   aboutItems.forEach(otherItem => {
│   │   │                       if (otherItem !== item) {
│   │   │                           otherItem.classList.remove('active');
│   │   │                       }
│   │   │                   });
│   │   │               });
│   │   │           });
│   │   │       
│   │   │           const staffMembers = document.querySelectorAll('.staff-member');
│   │   │       
│   │   │           staffMembers.forEach(member => {
│   │   │               member.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │   │                   const profile = member.nextElementSibling; // Get the corresponding profile section
│   │   │                   profile.classList.toggle('active'); // Toggle the active class to show/hide
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Optional: Close other profiles
│   │   │                   staffMembers.forEach(otherMember => {
│   │   │                       if (otherMember !== member) {
│   │   │                           const otherProfile = otherMember.nextElementSibling;
│   │   │                           otherProfile.classList.remove('active'); // Hide other profiles
│   │   │                       }
│   │   │                   });
│   │   │               });
│   │   │           });
│   │   │       });
│   │   │       --- End of about.js ---
│   │   │   ├── faq.js
│   │   │       --- Start of faq.js ---
│   │   │       document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
│   │   │           const faqItems = document.querySelectorAll('.faq-item');
│   │   │       
│   │   │           faqItems.forEach(item => {
│   │   │               const question = item.querySelector('.faq-question');
│   │   │       
│   │   │               question.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │   │                   // Toggle the active class
│   │   │                   item.classList.toggle('active');
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Close other open FAQ items (optional)
│   │   │                   faqItems.forEach(otherItem => {
│   │   │                       if (otherItem !== item) {
│   │   │                           otherItem.classList.remove('active');
│   │   │                       }
│   │   │                   });
│   │   │               });
│   │   │           });
│   │   │       });
│   │   │       --- End of faq.js ---
│   │   │   └── home.js
│   │   │       --- Start of home.js ---
│   │   │       document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
│   │   │           const menuLinks = document.querySelectorAll("#main-menu ul li a");
│   │   │           const sprite = document.querySelector(".matsu-sprite");
│   │   │           const tooltip = document.querySelector("#tooltip");
│   │   │           const bubbleContainer = document.querySelector(".bubble-container"); // Select the bubble container
│   │   │       
│   │   │           if (sprite && tooltip && bubbleContainer) {
│   │   │               const originalSrc = "assets/sprites/matsu1.webp";
│   │   │               const hoverSrc = "assets/sprites/matsu2.webp";
│   │   │               const preloadedImage = new Image();
│   │   │               preloadedImage.src = hoverSrc;
│   │   │       
│   │   │               const tooltipTexts = {
│   │   │                   "Mods": "Discover a variety of mods to your enjoyment!",
│   │   │                   "Submissions": "Submit your own mods and assets, and share them with the community!",
│   │   │                   "Assets": "Browse and download assets for your projects!",
│   │   │                   "Classroom": "Join our classroom to learn about RenPy, DDLC, and modding!",
│   │   │                   "About": "Learn more about Doki Doki Modding Central!",
│   │   │                   "FAQ": "Find answers to frequently asked questions!"
│   │   │               };
│   │   │       
│   │   │               let typingInterval = null; // Store the interval ID
│   │   │               let tooltipTimeout = null; // Store the timeout ID for hiding the tooltip
│   │   │       
│   │   │               /**
│   │   │                * Clears any existing typing interval and tooltip timeout.
│   │   │                */
│   │   │               const clearExistingTimers = () => {
│   │   │                   if (typingInterval) {
│   │   │                       clearInterval(typingInterval);
│   │   │                       typingInterval = null;
│   │   │                   }
│   │   │                   if (tooltipTimeout) {
│   │   │                       clearTimeout(tooltipTimeout);
│   │   │                       tooltipTimeout = null;
│   │   │                   }
│   │   │               };
│   │   │       
│   │   │               /**
│   │   │                * Types out the provided text into the tooltip element.
│   │   │                * @param {string} text - The text to type out.
│   │   │                */
│   │   │               const typeText = (text) => {
│   │   │                   clearExistingTimers(); // Ensure no overlapping intervals
│   │   │                   let index = 0;
│   │   │                   tooltip.textContent = ''; 
│   │   │                   tooltip.style.display = 'block'; 
│   │   │                   tooltip.classList.remove('hide');
│   │   │                   tooltip.classList.add('show');
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   typingInterval = setInterval(() => {
│   │   │                       if (index < text.length) {
│   │   │                           tooltip.textContent += text.charAt(index);
│   │   │                           index++;
│   │   │                       } else {
│   │   │                           clearExistingTimers();
│   │   │                       }
│   │   │                   }, 40); // Typing speed
│   │   │               };
│   │   │       
│   │   │               /**
│   │   │                * Handles the mouse enter and focus events on menu links.
│   │   │                * @param {Event} event - The event object.
│   │   │                */
│   │   │               const handleMouseEnter = (event) => {
│   │   │                   sprite.src = hoverSrc;
│   │   │                   const menuItem = event.target.textContent.trim();
│   │   │                   const tooltipText = tooltipTexts[menuItem] || `Information about ${menuItem}`;
│   │   │                   typeText(tooltipText);
│   │   │               };
│   │   │       
│   │   │               /**
│   │   │                * Handles the mouse leave and blur events on menu links.
│   │   │                */
│   │   │               const handleMouseLeave = () => {
│   │   │                   sprite.src = originalSrc;
│   │   │                   clearExistingTimers(); // Stop typing and clear timeouts
│   │   │                   tooltip.textContent = ''; // Clear the text immediately
│   │   │                   tooltip.classList.remove('show');
│   │   │                   tooltip.classList.add('hide');
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Set a timeout to hide the tooltip after a brief delay
│   │   │                   tooltipTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
│   │   │                       tooltip.style.display = 'none';
│   │   │                   }, 500); // Match the transition duration in CSS
│   │   │               };
│   │   │       
│   │   │               // Attach event listeners to each menu link
│   │   │               menuLinks.forEach(link => {
│   │   │                   link.addEventListener("mouseenter", handleMouseEnter);
│   │   │                   link.addEventListener("mouseleave", handleMouseLeave);
│   │   │                   link.addEventListener("focus", handleMouseEnter);
│   │   │                   link.addEventListener("blur", handleMouseLeave);
│   │   │               });
│   │   │       
│   │   │               // Bubble Effect Implementation
│   │   │       
│   │   │               const MAX_BUBBLES = 30; // Maximum number of bubbles on screen
│   │   │       
│   │   │               const createBubble = () => {
│   │   │                   if (bubbleContainer.children.length >= MAX_BUBBLES) return; // Limit the number of bubbles
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   const bubble = document.createElement('div');
│   │   │                   bubble.classList.add('bubble');
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Random size between 10px and 40px
│   │   │                   const size = Math.random() * 30 + 10;
│   │   │                   bubble.style.width = `${size}px`;
│   │   │                   bubble.style.height = `${size}px`;
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Random horizontal position (0% to 100%)
│   │   │                   const position = Math.random() * 100;
│   │   │                   bubble.style.left = `${position}%`;
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Random animation duration between 8s and 20s
│   │   │                   const duration = Math.random() * 12 + 8;
│   │   │                   bubble.style.animationDuration = `${duration}s`;
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Random opacity between 0.5 and 0.7 for variation
│   │   │                   const opacity = Math.random() * 0.2 + 0.5;
│   │   │                   bubble.style.backgroundColor = `rgba(255, 255, 255, ${opacity})`;
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Append the bubble to the container
│   │   │                   bubbleContainer.appendChild(bubble);
│   │   │       
│   │   │                   // Remove the bubble after the animation completes to prevent DOM clutter
│   │   │                   bubble.addEventListener('animationend', () => {
│   │   │                       bubble.remove();
│   │   │                   });
│   │   │               };
│   │   │       
│   │   │               // Create bubbles at intervals
│   │   │               const bubbleInterval = setInterval(createBubble, 1000); // Generate a bubble every 1 second
│   │   │           } else {
│   │   │               console.error("Sprite image with class 'matsu-sprite', tooltip with id 'tooltip', or bubble container not found.");
│   │   │           }
│   │   │       });
│   │   │       --- End of home.js ---
│   │   └── plugins.js
│   │       --- Start of plugins.js ---

│   │       --- End of plugins.js ---

├── [components]/
│   ├── addComponents.js
│       --- Start of addComponents.js ---
│       document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
│           // Load an HTML component and insert it into the DOM.
│           function loadComponent(url, insertPosition) {
│               fetch(url)
│                   .then(response => {
│                       if (!response.ok) {
│                           throw new Error(`Could not fetch ${url}: ${response.statusText}`);
│                       }
│                       return response.text();
│                   })
│                   .then(data => {
│                       if (insertPosition === 'prepend') {
│                           // Insert the component at the beginning of the body
│                           document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', data);
│                       } else if (insertPosition === 'append') {
│                           // Insert the component at the end of the body
│                           document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', data);
│                       }
│                   })
│                   .catch(error => {
│                       console.error('Error loading component:', error);
│                   });
│           }
│       
│           // Determine if the current page is the homepage
│           const path = window.location.pathname;
│           const isHomePage = path === '/' || path.endsWith('/index.html');
│       
│           // If it's not the homepage, load the header and footer
│           if (!isHomePage) {
│               loadComponent('/components/header/header.html', 'prepend');
│               loadComponent('/components/footer/footer.html', 'append');
│           }
│       });
│       --- End of addComponents.js ---

│           --- Start of header.css ---
│           /* Header Background with Soft Linear Gradient */
│           header {
│               position: relative; /* Establish positioning context for overlay */
│               padding: 20px 0;
│               background: linear-gradient(90deg, #3CB371, #FF7F7F, #DDA0DD, #FFB6C1); /* Softer colors */
│               overflow: hidden; /* Prevent overflow from pseudo-elements */
│           }
│           
│           /* Semi-Transparent Overlay */
│           header::before {
│               content: '';
│               position: absolute;
│               top: 0;
│               left: 0;
│               width: 100%;
│               height: 100%;
│               background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.2); /* Black with 20% opacity */
│               z-index: 1; /* Position behind the navbar content */
│               pointer-events: none; /* Allow clicks to pass through */
│           }
│           
│           /* Navbar Container Positioning */
│           header nav {
│               position: relative; /* Stacking context */
│               z-index: 2; /* Position above the overlay */
│           }
│           
│           /* Navbar List Styling */
│           header nav ul {
│               list-style: none;
│               display: flex;
│               justify-content: center;
│               align-items: center; /* Vertically center the navbar */
│               margin: 0;
│               padding: 0;
│           }
│           
│           /* Navbar Items Spacing */
│           header nav ul li {
│               margin: 0 15px;
│           }
│           
│           /* Navbar Links Styling */
│           header nav ul li a {
│               color: #ffffff;
│               text-decoration: none;
│               font-size: 18px;
│               font-family: 'HotMustardBTNRegular', sans-serif;
│               transition: color 0.3s ease, text-decoration 0.3s ease;
│               text-shadow: 1px 1px 2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5); /* Subtle shadow */
│           }
│           
│           /* Active Navbar Link Styling */
│           header nav ul li a.active {
│               text-decoration: underline;
│               color: #ff00d4; /* Magenta color for active link */
│           }
│           
│           /* Navbar Links Hover Effect */
│           header nav ul li a:hover {
│               text-decoration: underline;
│               color: #bd02ae; /* Slightly darker magenta color on hover for better UX */
│           }

│               <section id="about-container">
│                   <h1>About Doki Doki Modding Central</h1>
│       
│                   <div class="about-section">
│                       <button class="about-question">What We Are</button>
│                       <div class="about-answer">
│                       <p>
│                           Doki Doki Modding Central is an all-encompassing fan modification emporium for modifying <em>Doki Doki Literature Club!</em> by Team Salvato. Made by a handful of individuals with years of experience in the DDLC modding scene, this website is made in hopes to provide a space for the consumption, exploration, critique, and creation of modifications for the franchise. This initiative is cultivated by providing a repository of mods, new and republished, regardless of petty internet drama or stigma. Alongside this, we wish to provide the resources necessary to generate new content for the franchise and give a foot in the door for new entrants into game creation. The implementation of a Discord server for discussion of modifications hopes to achieve a ground of active communication and attributing to the betterment of mod creation and story-telling, meanwhile giving a place for fans to discuss amongst themselves and provide crucial feedback on works that the authors can partake in.
│                       </p>
│                   </div>
│                   </div>
│       
│                   <div class="about-section">
│                       <button class="about-question">What We Stand By</button>
│                       <div class="about-answer">
│                       <p>
│                           This website was born out of a kindling of hope in October of 2023 by Savage Sentral, Tune Eternal, and JayQilin. Formerly members of the subreddit, <a href="https://www.reddit.com/r/DDLCmods" target="_blank"><strong>r/DDLCmods</strong></a>, better known as the Doki Doki Modding Community, these three deliberated the idea of creating a website independent from the subreddit to restore a sense of self to the original idea of modding Doki Doki Literature Club: to foster fun.
│                       </p>
│                       <p>
│                           Over the course of three years between 2021 and 2023, these three quickly gained notoriety in the grander modding community and main DDLC community by extension. What for, you may be asking? The reason is simple: for calling out the lack of care for the community members. Savage Sentral, lead creator of the website, is a content creator best known for the documentation and journalistic reporting of ongoing dramas in the community. Whether it is exposing creeps and pedophiles, reporting on bizarre happenings, and generally informing the public to what is occurring in the modding scene, Savage Sentral stands as a vanguard for the safety of the modding community. Savage Sentral would initially get in contact with Tune Eternal, JayQilin, and site developer/admin/owner, L4w1i3t, in October of 2022 at the peak of the former existence of Team Red Mazda RX-7 (STOCK), which would kindle a close friendship eventually leading to where we are today.
│                       </p>
│                       <p>
│                           It was through the destruction of Team Red Mazda RX-7 (STOCK) that solidified our virtues. During this time and in the year after, it was seen that there was deeply-seated corruption at every step in the Doki Doki Modding Community. Not only this, but an observable lack of care, understanding, and intelligence, too. Under the guise of justice and a fair application of the law, the moderators of the subreddit threw out their only investigator into the drama, L4w1i3t. When reaching out over concerns relating to mental health and wellbeing, the administrators showed pure hostility in asking for their aid. And when asked for a whole week while the drama transpired to take action against the troublemakers perpetuating it, they instead did everything in their power to smite the victims. It was through this drama that repercussions are still felt to this day in the modding community as a whole. Quarantine of the subreddit requires the pre-approval of posts, suspicion of alternative accounts at every turn, and deletion of content or posts for anything that might show any slight deviation from whatever approved narrative the administration has. All of that is due to what happened in October 2022.
│                       </p>
│                       <p>
│                           Throughout 2023, the site founders partook in thorough investigation spanning the entirety of the life of the modding community to determine the failings of that drama. The suspected originators of the drama, which the administrators were made aware of at the time, revealed themselves months later as being the ones to start it, having the inaction of the admins being the cause of a whole mod team being disintegrated. The administrators having a heavy hand in censorship, while having a past uncleansed revealing lack of sympathy for the mentally distressed and suicidal. Favoritism too being the cause of inaction, as key members of a well-known mod team being the sole culprits, one of which being a pedophile, had sketchy opinions in favor of them shown by existing moderators. Founder of DokiMods.me, ItsZekrom, using alternative accounts to run defense for said pedophile. And despite all of this, every founder of this site was banned for voicing concern and attempting to help, alongside everyone in association with them found in their midst.
│                       </p>
│                       <p>
│                           And it wasn't just here that this downfall originated, in the past, there were many years worth of trouble in the modding scene. From splinter cells of former moderators attempting to co-opt the main community with another subreddit, to their founder being accused of pedophilia, to high-profile mod creators having unfair treatment applied to them by overbearing enforcement, and so much more. There is not a single moment in the rich history of the modding community that isn't rife with drama, and the people leading the charge against it show that they only get worse and worse at handling it.
│                       </p>
│                       <p>
│                           With this in mind, with what we here at DDMC have experienced firsthand, we have come to a set of rules of which we hold true. A framework of understanding that anyone visiting this site should be able to see weaved into every fiber of its being, as careful thought and care was put into every moment of it.
│                       </p>
│                   </div>
│                   </div>
│       
│                   <div class="about-section">
│                       <button class="about-question">What We Offer</button>
│                       <div class="about-answer">
│                       <p>
│                           Our platform provides an array of resources and features to cater to the community of DDLC modders and enthusiasts. Here's what you'll find on our site:
│                       </p>
│                       <ul>
│                           <li><strong>FAQ:</strong> Access a set of frequently asked questions to assist both newcomers and veterans in navigating the platform and addressing common queries.</li>
│                           <li><strong>MOD CATALOGS &amp; ARCHIVE:</strong> Discover and explore an extensive catalog of mods available for various platforms, including Windows, Mac, Linux, and specifically curated mods compatible with Android devices. We aim to showcase a diverse range of these creations, including the good, the bad, and the ugly.</li>
│                           <li><strong>ASSETS REPOSITORY:</strong> Access a curated collection of assets essential for mod creation, including but not limited to music, artwork, code snippets, and other resources to facilitate the modding process.</li>
│                           <li><strong>CHARACTER DATABASE:</strong> Explore a repository featuring a spectrum of characters usable within mods, encompassing original characters (OCs), poses, outfits, and additional resources that aid in character customization and storytelling.</li>
│                           <li><strong>RENPY DOCUMENTATION AND TUTORIALS:</strong> Access comprehensive documentation, guides, and tutorials specifically tailored to Ren'Py, the visual novel engine used for creating DDLC mods. These resources aim to assist modders at all levels in leveraging Ren'Py's functionalities effectively.</li>
│                       </ul>
│                       <p>
│                           Our commitment is to offer a definitive platform that not only hosts mods but also fosters creativity, collaboration, and enjoyment within the DDLC modding community. Should you have any questions about our offerings or site content, please don't hesitate to reach out to us for prompt assistance.
│                       </p>
│                   </div>
│                   </div>
│       
│                   <div class="about-section">
│                       <button class="about-question">What We Enforce</button>
│                       <div class="about-answer">
│                       <p>Let's lay out the ground rules:</p>
│                       <ol>
│                           <li>
│                               <strong>Archive EVERYTHING:</strong>
│                               Unlike its contemporary, DDMC wishes to offer a platform in which everyone can express themselves and put their hard work out there: past, present, and future. With this, no stone goes unturned. This is a library of all mods and wishes that everyone gets their time to shine, no matter what someone has to say about them. With this too, no one should have to suffer FOMO from the removal of a mod, so mods removed due to controversy should also be posted here. Like stated before, archive EVERYTHING.
│                               <ul>
│                                   <li>
│                                       <strong>1a.</strong> All mod creations are accepted and will be published. This includes mods including copyrighted materials. It should be your responsibility to uphold the copyright law of your respective country, understand the copyright policies of external content sites like YouTube, as well as follow the <a href="http://teamsalvato.com/ip-guidelines/" target="_blank"><strong>Team Salvato IP Guidelines</strong></a>. We will not enforce action against the individuals violating any of these and are not responsible by proxy for any infringements. It is up to the original holders of respective IPs to reach out to the individuals that used the materials wrongly on a discretionary basis. So if any of this is confusing to a fellow mod creator, simply put, negligence of the law does not make you exempt from it. Make everyone's life easier by taking the proper precautions before publishing new creations.
│                                   </li>
│                               </ul>
│                           </li>
│                           <li>
│                               <strong>Don't Publish Anything Illegal or Maliciously Offensive (To Your Respective Jurisdiction):</strong>
│                               Does this really need explaining?
│                           </li>
│                           <li>
│                               <strong>Have Fun:</strong>
│                               This is a portal for the expansion of a video game after all. The main focus should always be for your enjoyment. If you wish to post here, know that you are contributing to the greater enjoyment of others and that everyone that comes across your projects and contributions will be grateful for them. It is no one's right to take that away from you.
│                           </li>
│                       </ol>
│                   </div>
│                   </div>

│       <!DOCTYPE html>

│           <title>FAQ - Doki Doki Modding Central</title>
│           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../assets/css/styles.css">
│           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../components/header/header.css">
│           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../components/footer/footer.css">

│               <section id="faq-container">
│                   <h1>Frequently Asked Questions</h1>
│       
│                   <div class="faq-section">
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">TL;DR What is Doki Doki Modding Central?</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>TL;DR Doki Doki Modding Central (DDMC) is a comprehensive sister platform dedicated to creating, sharing, and 
│                                   exploring modifications for <em>Doki Doki Literature Club!</em> by Team Salvato. It serves as a hub 
│                                   for modders and fans to collaborate, share resources, and enhance their experience.</p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│       
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">How can I submit my mod to DDMC?</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>We have two specific Google Forms that you can access by going to their respective pages. You can submit your
│                                   mod by filling out the mod submission form with all the requisite information. The other form is where you
│                                   can submit assets (music, code, sprites, art, etc.) to be uploaded for others to use.
│                               </p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│       
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">Are there any rules for creating mods?</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>Yes, although we try to be as hands-off as we can; we're not an anarchy, but we also don't rule with an iron fist 
│                                   either. See the "About" page for what we do enforce.</p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│       
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">Do I need any specific software to create a mod?</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>While the specific tools depend on the type of mod you're creating, most DDLC mods are developed using 
│                                   the Ren'Py engine. We provide comprehensive documentation and tutorials in the classroom to help you 
│                                   get started, if you need help, or if you want to learn anything new.</p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│       
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">How can I get involved in the community?</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>Getting involved in the community can be as simple as contributing your thoughts and ideas--it makes a big 
│                                   difference and supports everyone here. If you'd like to take a more active role, you can connect with staff 
│                                   and other members through our subreddit or Discord server. For those interested in joining the team, we 
│                                   announce open positions whenever we're hiring. If you're passionate and interested, let us know! We value 
│                                   merit and commitment above all else.
│                               </p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│       
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">Is there support available if I encounter issues?</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>Absolutely! Not only do we have a dedicated feedback form and channel in the Discord server, where you can either
│                                   be anonymous or known. You can also reach out to one of the staff members directly if you so choose. Also note that
│                                   feedback is not just exclusive to technical issues; your complaints can also be about anything that may impact the
│                                   community negatively if left unchecked--harrassment by other users, abuse of power by a staff member, grooming,
│                                   you name it. We value all input regardless of significance.
│                               </p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│       
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">I'm not allowed in the subreddit/Discord server, can I still upload mods?</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>
│                                   Keep in mind: we actually don't ban people from the Discord server, only with particularly egregious exceptions;
│                                   see the server to find out what we do instead. As for uploading mods as a banned user, you absolutely can, as per rule
│                                   1 on the "About" page. We like to separate art from artist here.
│                               </p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│                       
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">My mod wasn't made with Ren'Py. Can it still be added to the site?</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>
│                                   Yes, you can submit your mods regardless of engine or how you made it. Be advised that during your submission, you
│                                   will have to outline how exactly to install and run it, as it would deviate from the standard instructions.
│                                   Also remember that your mod <strong>does</strong> have to be complicit with Team Salvato's IP Guidelines, so
│                                   you can't submit a pre-installed/pre-built mod. We don't make the rules, we just enforce them.
│                               </p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│       
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">My mod's not on the site yet, and I submitted it days ago!</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>
│                                   Please have patience. We have at most two people right now that manage the site--one is a busy IT specialist, and
│                                   the other is a busy university student. Point is, we do have lives, and we will upload mods and assets whenever
│                                   we have the chance to. As such, we also prefer to upload in massive batches instead of on an individual basis,
│                                   so be assured that you're not the only one thinking this. TL;DR we'll get to your stuff eventually.
│                               </p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│       
│                       <div class="faq-item">
│                           <button class="faq-question">Who's Matsuda?</button>
│                           <div class="faq-answer">
│                               <p>
│                                   She's a totally real person who does totally real things. Source: trust me bro.
│                               </p>
│                           </div>
│                       </div>
│

│   │   ├── android.html
│   │       --- Start of android.html ---
│   │       <!DOCTYPE html>
│   │       <html lang="en">
│   │       <head>
│   │           <meta charset="UTF-8">
│   │           <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
│   │           <title>Android Mods - Doki Doki Modding Central</title>
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../assets/css/styles.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../components/header/header.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../components/footer/footer.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../assets/css/page_specific/android.css">
│   │           <link rel="icon" href="../../assets/gui/favicon.ico" type="image/x-icon">
│   │       </head>
│   │       <body>
│   │       
│   │       <main>
│   │           <section id="mods-container">
│   │               <h1>Android Mods</h1>
│   │               <div id="mods-list" class="mod-grid"></div>
│   │               <div id="pagination-controls" class="pagination">
│   │                   <button id="prev-page" disabled>Previous</button>
│   │                   <span id="page-info">Page 1</span>
│   │                   <button id="next-page">Next</button>
│   │               </div>
│   │           </section>
│   │       </main>
│   │       
│   │       <script>
│   │           const itemsPerPage = 16;
│   │           let currentPage = 1;
│   │           let totalPages = 1;
│   │           let allMods = [];
│   │       
│   │           const container = document.getElementById('mods-list');
│   │           const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prev-page');
│   │           const nextBtn = document.getElementById('next-page');
│   │           const pageInfo = document.getElementById('page-info');
│   │       
│   │           function renderPage(pageNumber) {
│   │               container.innerHTML = '';
│   │               const startIndex = (pageNumber - 1) * itemsPerPage;
│   │               const endIndex = startIndex + itemsPerPage;
│   │               const modsToShow = allMods.slice(startIndex, endIndex);
│   │       
│   │               modsToShow.forEach(mod => {
│   │                   const modCard = document.createElement('a');
│   │                   modCard.classList.add('mod-card');
│   │                   modCard.href = `./android/${mod.route}/mod.html`;
│   │                   modCard.innerHTML = `
│   │                       <img src="${mod.imageUrl}" alt="${mod.title}" class="mod-image" />
│   │                       <h2>${mod.title}</h2>
│   │                       <p>By: ${mod.author}</p>
│   │                   `;
│   │                   container.appendChild(modCard);
│   │               });
│   │       
│   │               pageInfo.textContent = `Page ${pageNumber} of ${totalPages}`;
│   │               prevBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === 1);
│   │               nextBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === totalPages);
│   │           }
│   │       
│   │           fetch('../../data/mods.json')
│   │               .then(response => response.json())
│   │               .then(data => {
│   │                   allMods = data.android;
│   │                   const totalItems = allMods.length;
│   │                   totalPages = Math.ceil(totalItems / itemsPerPage);
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               })
│   │               .catch(error => console.error('Error loading mods:', error));
│   │       
│   │           prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage > 1) {
│   │                   currentPage--;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       
│   │           nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage < totalPages) {
│   │                   currentPage++;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       </script>
│   │       
│   │       <script src="../../components/addComponents.js"></script>
│   │       <script src="../../assets/js/main.js"></script>
│   │       </body>
│   │       </html>
│   │       --- End of android.html ---
│   │   ├── [archive]/

│   │   ├── archive.html
│   │       --- Start of archive.html ---
│   │       <!DOCTYPE html>
│   │       <html lang="en">
│   │       <head>
│   │           <meta charset="UTF-8">
│   │           <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
│   │           <title>Mod Archive - Doki Doki Modding Central</title>
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../assets/css/styles.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../components/header/header.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../components/footer/footer.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../assets/css/page_specific/archive.css">
│   │           <link rel="icon" href="../../assets/gui/favicon.ico" type="image/x-icon">
│   │       </head>
│   │       <body>
│   │       
│   │       <main>
│   │           <section id="mods-container">
│   │               <h1>Mod Archive</h1>
│   │               <div id="mods-list" class="mod-grid"></div>
│   │               <div id="pagination-controls" class="pagination">
│   │                   <button id="prev-page" disabled>Previous</button>
│   │                   <span id="page-info">Page 1</span>
│   │                   <button id="next-page">Next</button>
│   │               </div>
│   │           </section>
│   │       </main>
│   │       
│   │       <script>
│   │           const itemsPerPage = 16;
│   │           let currentPage = 1;
│   │           let totalPages = 1;
│   │           let allMods = [];
│   │       
│   │           const container = document.getElementById('mods-list');
│   │           const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prev-page');
│   │           const nextBtn = document.getElementById('next-page');
│   │           const pageInfo = document.getElementById('page-info');
│   │       
│   │           function renderPage(pageNumber) {
│   │               container.innerHTML = '';
│   │               const startIndex = (pageNumber - 1) * itemsPerPage;
│   │               const endIndex = startIndex + itemsPerPage;
│   │               const modsToShow = allMods.slice(startIndex, endIndex);
│   │       
│   │               modsToShow.forEach(mod => {
│   │                   const modCard = document.createElement('a');
│   │                   modCard.classList.add('mod-card');
│   │                   modCard.href = `./archive/${mod.route}/mod.html`;
│   │                   modCard.innerHTML = `
│   │                       <img src="${mod.imageUrl}" alt="${mod.title}" class="mod-image" />
│   │                       <h2>${mod.title}</h2>
│   │                       <p>By: ${mod.author}</p>
│   │                   `;
│   │                   container.appendChild(modCard);
│   │               });
│   │       
│   │               pageInfo.textContent = `Page ${pageNumber} of ${totalPages}`;
│   │               prevBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === 1);
│   │               nextBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === totalPages);
│   │           }
│   │       
│   │           fetch('../../data/mods.json')
│   │               .then(response => response.json())
│   │               .then(data => {
│   │                   allMods = data.archive;
│   │                   const totalItems = allMods.length;
│   │                   totalPages = Math.ceil(totalItems / itemsPerPage);
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               })
│   │               .catch(error => console.error('Error loading mods:', error));
│   │       
│   │           prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage > 1) {
│   │                   currentPage--;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       
│   │           nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage < totalPages) {
│   │                   currentPage++;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       </script>
│   │       
│   │       <script src="../../components/addComponents.js"></script>
│   │       <script src="../../assets/js/main.js"></script>
│   │       </body>
│   │       </html>
│   │       --- End of archive.html ---
│   │   ├── [demos]/

│   │   ├── demos.html
│   │       --- Start of demos.html ---
│   │       <!DOCTYPE html>
│   │       <html lang="en">
│   │       <head>
│   │           <meta charset="UTF-8">
│   │           <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
│   │           <title>Mod Demos - Doki Doki Modding Central</title>
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../assets/css/styles.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../components/header/header.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../components/footer/footer.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../assets/css/page_specific/demos.css">
│   │           <link rel="icon" href="../../assets/gui/favicon.ico" type="image/x-icon">
│   │       </head>
│   │       <body>
│   │       
│   │       <main>
│   │           <section id="mods-container">
│   │               <h1>Mod Demos</h1>
│   │               <div id="mods-list" class="mod-grid"></div>
│   │               <div id="pagination-controls" class="pagination">
│   │                   <button id="prev-page" disabled>Previous</button>
│   │                   <span id="page-info">Page 1</span>
│   │                   <button id="next-page">Next</button>
│   │               </div>
│   │           </section>
│   │       </main>
│   │       
│   │       <script>
│   │           const itemsPerPage = 16;
│   │           let currentPage = 1;
│   │           let totalPages = 1;
│   │           let allMods = [];
│   │       
│   │           const container = document.getElementById('mods-list');
│   │           const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prev-page');
│   │           const nextBtn = document.getElementById('next-page');
│   │           const pageInfo = document.getElementById('page-info');
│   │       
│   │           function renderPage(pageNumber) {
│   │               container.innerHTML = '';
│   │               const startIndex = (pageNumber - 1) * itemsPerPage;
│   │               const endIndex = startIndex + itemsPerPage;
│   │               const modsToShow = allMods.slice(startIndex, endIndex);
│   │       
│   │               modsToShow.forEach(mod => {
│   │                   const modCard = document.createElement('a');
│   │                   modCard.classList.add('mod-card');
│   │                   modCard.href = `./demos/${mod.route}/mod.html`;
│   │                   modCard.innerHTML = `
│   │                       <img src="${mod.imageUrl}" alt="${mod.title}" class="mod-image" />
│   │                       <h2>${mod.title}</h2>
│   │                       <p>By: ${mod.author}</p>
│   │                   `;
│   │                   container.appendChild(modCard);
│   │               });
│   │       
│   │               pageInfo.textContent = `Page ${pageNumber} of ${totalPages}`;
│   │               prevBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === 1);
│   │               nextBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === totalPages);
│   │           }
│   │       
│   │           fetch('../../data/mods.json')
│   │               .then(response => response.json())
│   │               .then(data => {
│   │                   allMods = data.demos;
│   │                   const totalItems = allMods.length;
│   │                   totalPages = Math.ceil(totalItems / itemsPerPage);
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               })
│   │               .catch(error => console.error('Error loading mods:', error));
│   │       
│   │           prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage > 1) {
│   │                   currentPage--;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       
│   │           nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage < totalPages) {
│   │                   currentPage++;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       </script>
│   │       
│   │       <script src="../../components/addComponents.js"></script>
│   │       <script src="../../assets/js/main.js"></script>
│   │       </body>
│   │       </html>
│   │       --- End of demos.html ---
│   │   ├── populate_modhtml.py
│   │       --- Start of populate_modhtml.py ---
│   │       import os
│   │       
│   │       HTML_TEMPLATE = """<!DOCTYPE html>
│   │       <html lang="en">
│   │       <head>
│   │           <meta charset="UTF-8">
│   │           <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
│   │           <title>[MOD TITLE] - Doki Doki Modding Central</title>
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../../../assets/css/styles.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../../../components/header/header.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../../../components/footer/footer.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../../../assets/css/mod_style.css">
│   │           <link rel="icon" href="../../../../assets/gui/favicon.ico" type="image/x-icon">
│   │       </head>
│   │       <body>
│   │       
│   │           <main>
│   │               <section id="mod-container">
│   │                   <div class="mod-content">
│   │                       <h1>[MOD TITLE]</h1>
│   │                       <img src="../../../../assets/mod_prevs/[image].webp" alt="Mod Preview" class="mod-image">
│   │                       <p><strong>Author:</strong> [AUTHOR]</p>
│   │                       <p><strong>Description:</strong></p>
│   │                       <p>[insert description here]</p>
│   │                       <div class="mod-download">
│   │                           <a href="link_to_download" class="download-button">Download Mod</a>
│   │                       </div>
│   │                   </div>
│   │               </section>
│   │           </main>
│   │       
│   │           <script src="../../../../components/addComponents.js"></script>
│   │           <script src="../../../../assets/js/main.js"></script>
│   │       </body>
│   │       </html>
│   │       """
│   │       
│   │       BASE_DIR = "."
│   │       
│   │       def populate_empty_mods(base_dir):
│   │           for root, _, files in os.walk(base_dir):
│   │               for file in files:
│   │                   if file == "mod.html":
│   │                       file_path = os.path.join(root, file)
│   │                       # Check if the file is empty
│   │                       if os.path.getsize(file_path) == 0:
│   │                           print(f"Populating empty file: {file_path}")
│   │                           with open(file_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
│   │                               f.write(HTML_TEMPLATE)
│   │       
│   │       if __name__ == "__main__":
│   │           populate_empty_mods(BASE_DIR)
│   │           print("Script execution complete.")
│   │       --- End of populate_modhtml.py ---

│   │   │   │                       <img src="../../../../assets/mod_prevs/brokenpoet.webp" alt="Mod Preview" class="mod-image">

│   │   │   │                       <p><strong>Description:</strong></p>
│   │   │   │                       <p>The festival has passed. All 4 girls read their poems, but no one really cared. At least at the end of the day, 
│   │   │   │                           everyone seems proud they kept to their vision of what the club should be. Sayori is happy you joined the club, 
│   │   │   │                           but despite that, you haven't really connected with anyone new. Her puppy eyes are too much to bear, and you 
│   │   │   │                           reluctantly promise to try and get to know the other members of the club better. Natsuki in particular is puzzling. 
│   │   │   │                           You can't really put a finger on why she continues to come to club despite seemingly not really getting along with 
│   │   │   │                           anyone, and that is somewhat intriguing. Maybe you can break the ice with her... Maybe you can be her friend. 
│   │   │   │                           Maybe something more.</p>

│   │   ├── standard.html
│   │       --- Start of standard.html ---
│   │       <!DOCTYPE html>
│   │       <html lang="en">
│   │       <head>
│   │           <meta charset="UTF-8">
│   │           <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
│   │           <title>Standard Mods - Doki Doki Modding Central</title>
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../assets/css/styles.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../components/header/header.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../components/footer/footer.css">
│   │           <link rel="stylesheet" href="../../assets/css/page_specific/standard.css">
│   │           <link rel="icon" href="../../assets/gui/favicon.ico" type="image/x-icon">
│   │       </head>
│   │       <body>
│   │       
│   │       <main>
│   │           <section id="mods-container">
│   │               <h1>Standard Mods</h1>
│   │               <div id="mods-list" class="mod-grid"></div>
│   │               <div id="pagination-controls" class="pagination">
│   │                   <button id="prev-page" disabled>Previous</button>
│   │                   <span id="page-info">Page 1</span>
│   │                   <button id="next-page">Next</button>
│   │               </div>
│   │           </section>
│   │       </main>
│   │       
│   │       <script>
│   │           const itemsPerPage = 16;
│   │           let currentPage = 1;
│   │           let totalPages = 1;
│   │           let allMods = [];
│   │       
│   │           const container = document.getElementById('mods-list');
│   │           const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prev-page');
│   │           const nextBtn = document.getElementById('next-page');
│   │           const pageInfo = document.getElementById('page-info');
│   │       
│   │           function renderPage(pageNumber) {
│   │               container.innerHTML = '';
│   │               const startIndex = (pageNumber - 1) * itemsPerPage;
│   │               const endIndex = startIndex + itemsPerPage;
│   │               const modsToShow = allMods.slice(startIndex, endIndex);
│   │       
│   │               modsToShow.forEach(mod => {
│   │                   const modCard = document.createElement('a');
│   │                   modCard.classList.add('mod-card');
│   │                   modCard.href = `./standard/${mod.route}/mod.html`;
│   │                   modCard.innerHTML = `
│   │                       <img src="${mod.imageUrl}" alt="${mod.title}" class="mod-image" />
│   │                       <h2>${mod.title}</h2>
│   │                       <p>By: ${mod.author}</p>
│   │                   `;
│   │                   container.appendChild(modCard);
│   │               });
│   │       
│   │               pageInfo.textContent = `Page ${pageNumber} of ${totalPages}`;
│   │               prevBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === 1);
│   │               nextBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === totalPages);
│   │           }
│   │       
│   │           fetch('../../data/mods.json')
│   │               .then(response => response.json())
│   │               .then(data => {
│   │                   allMods = data.standard;
│   │                   const totalItems = allMods.length;
│   │                   totalPages = Math.ceil(totalItems / itemsPerPage);
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               })
│   │               .catch(error => console.error('Error loading mods:', error));
│   │       
│   │           prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage > 1) {
│   │                   currentPage--;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       
│   │           nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage < totalPages) {
│   │                   currentPage++;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       </script>
│   │       
│   │       <script src="../../components/addComponents.js"></script>
│   │       <script src="../../assets/js/main.js"></script>
│   │       </body>
│   │       </html>
│   │       --- End of standard.html ---
│   │   ├── [videos]/

│   │               <div id="mods-list" class="mod-grid"></div>
│   │               <div id="pagination-controls" class="pagination">
│   │                   <button id="prev-page" disabled>Previous</button>
│   │                   <span id="page-info">Page 1</span>
│   │                   <button id="next-page">Next</button>
│   │               </div>
│   │           </section>
│   │       </main>
│   │       
│   │       <script>
│   │           const itemsPerPage = 16;
│   │           let currentPage = 1;
│   │           let totalPages = 1;
│   │           let allMods = [];
│   │       
│   │           const container = document.getElementById('mods-list');
│   │           const prevBtn = document.getElementById('prev-page');
│   │           const nextBtn = document.getElementById('next-page');
│   │           const pageInfo = document.getElementById('page-info');
│   │       
│   │           function renderPage(pageNumber) {
│   │               container.innerHTML = '';
│   │               const startIndex = (pageNumber - 1) * itemsPerPage;
│   │               const endIndex = startIndex + itemsPerPage;
│   │               const modsToShow = allMods.slice(startIndex, endIndex);
│   │       
│   │               modsToShow.forEach(mod => {
│   │                   const modCard = document.createElement('a');
│   │                   modCard.classList.add('mod-card');
│   │                   modCard.href = `./videos/${mod.route}/mod.html`;
│   │                   modCard.innerHTML = `
│   │                       <img src="${mod.imageUrl}" alt="${mod.title}" class="mod-image" />
│   │                       <h2>${mod.title}</h2>
│   │                       <p>By: ${mod.author}</p>
│   │                   `;
│   │                   container.appendChild(modCard);
│   │               });
│   │       
│   │               pageInfo.textContent = `Page ${pageNumber} of ${totalPages}`;
│   │               prevBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === 1);
│   │               nextBtn.disabled = (pageNumber === totalPages);
│   │           }
│   │       
│   │           fetch('../../data/mods.json')
│   │               .then(response => response.json())
│   │               .then(data => {
│   │                   allMods = data.videos;
│   │                   const totalItems = allMods.length;
│   │                   totalPages = Math.ceil(totalItems / itemsPerPage);
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               })
│   │               .catch(error => console.error('Error loading mods:', error));
│   │       
│   │           prevBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage > 1) {
│   │                   currentPage--;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       
│   │           nextBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
│   │               if (currentPage < totalPages) {
│   │                   currentPage++;
│   │                   renderPage(currentPage);
│   │               }
│   │           });
│   │       </script>
│   │       
│   │       <script src="../../components/addComponents.js"></script>
│   │       <script src="../../assets/js/main.js"></script>
│   │       </body>
│   │       </html>
│   │       --- End of videos.html ---
